<title>Scope</title>
<p id="_ab28fb11-e5bd-ffbc-2e46-207f6c65db0f">This OGC Standard for Designing and Writing Modular Standards, also known as the <tt>ModSpec</tt>:</p>

000863cls-8
Hanging paragraph in clause
<clause id="cls-8" obligation="normative">
<title>ModSpec Requirements Class: Core</title>
<p id="_3939304b-c9fa-6f40-e291-a078e95e1bc0">This clause specifies the requirements and recommendations for the content and structure of a modular standard.
This collection of requirements, recommendations, and permissions are also known as the <tt>core</tt> of the ModSpec.
All the requirements specified in this ModSpec core comprise the ModSpec Core Requirements Class.</p>
2

<title>General Requirements</title>
<p id="_fa2fbadc-c9b2-7f08-39ec-135ef3932ce9">The following requirement states that every requirement in a standards document is associated with one or more requirements class(es).</p>

001224req_​imported-requirements-class
